Vehicle: 2026 Chevrolet Silverado 1500

Vehicle type: TRUCK

Trim: LT

Trim code: 1LT3

Drive types: 2WD, 4WD

Guide category: Colour and trim

Source tabs: Colour and Trim 3

Guide notes:

  • Requires (CXH) Leather Package.
  • On 1WT models requires (A2X) 10-way power driver seat adjuster. Not available with (ZW9) pickup bed delete.
  • Not available on Regular Cab models.
  • Note: GM will require 5 orders before sending to the plant. May require extended lead time.
